/* returns the value of the name cookie */
function readCookie(name) {
var nameEQ = name + "=";
var ca = document.cookie.split(';');
for(var i=0;i < ca.length;i++) {
var c = ca[i];
while (c.charAt(0)==' ') c = c.substring(1,c.length);
if (c.indexOf(nameEQ) == 0)
if (c.indexOf(nameEQ) == 0) return c.substring(nameEQ.length,c.length);
}
}

function getfeatures(id,mp,yextTagId, listingNumber) {
var hc = false;
var inx = 0;
var yextTagDivArray = $("div[id=yext-tag" + yextTagId+"]");
//var yextag = $("#yext-tag" + id).clone();
var yextag = $(yextTagDivArray[0]).clone();
var features = $("<div class='coupons'></div>");
if(id != 0){
if($("#fl" + id).length == 1){
var morefeat = $("#mofe" + id).clone();
features = $(features).append($("#fl" + id).clone());
$('li',features).each(function(index) {
inx = index + 1;
if((yextag.length == 1 && morefeat)){ hc=true; }
if ($(this).is("#coupon" + id) || $(this).is("#of" + id))
{
$(this).css("float","left"); $(this).css("display","block"); $(this).css("margin-left","-2px"); hc=true;
} else { $(this).remove(); }
});
if(inx > 0){ fltp = 3; }
if(morefeat && mp!=1){
$(morefeat.html()).appendTo($(features));
}
if(!hc && !yextag){ $("#dmf" + id).remove(); }
$(".feature-links",features).css("margin","0");
$(".feature-links",features).css("padding","0");
}
}else{
/* when pinTag value is not available for a listing,
at that mofe and f1 div is not renedering with proper id in listingpage.links.jsf.
For that reason it's require to retrieve mofe and f1 div as a children of mpbtm div.
*/
var morefeat = $("#mpbtm" + listingNumber).children("div.coupons").children("#mofe");
var fl = $("#mpbtm" + listingNumber).children("div.coupons").children("#fl");
features = $(features).append($(fl).clone());
$('li',features).each(function(index) {
inx = index + 1;
if((yextag.length == 1 && morefeat)){ hc=true; }
if ($(this).is("#coupon") || $(this).is("#of"))
{
$(this).css("float","left"); $(this).css("display","block"); $(this).css("margin-left","-2px"); hc=true;
} else { $(this).remove(); }
});
if(inx > 0){ fltp = 3; }
if(morefeat && mp!=1){
$(morefeat.html()).appendTo($(features));
}
if(!hc && !yextag){
$("#dmf" + (listingNumber+1)).remove();
}
$(".feature-links",features).css("margin","0");
$(".feature-links",features).css("padding","0");
}
if(yextag){
$(".yext-t",yextag).css("margin","4px 0 0 0");
$(".yext-t",yextag).css("float","left");
$(".yext-t",yextag).css("display","block");
$(".yextall",yextag).css("display","none");
$(".yexttrim",yextag).css("display","block");
$(yextag.html()).prependTo($(features));
}
if($("#fl" + id).length == 1 || yextag){
return features.html();
} else {
return;
}
}

}

}
}
}

function distLink () {

var ppvalue = '';

ppvalue = "&PP=L";
}

if (rr != 'AA'){ rrvalue = '&local=on&RR='+rr; }
var urlaa='http://yellowpages.superpages.com/listings.jsp?C=petsmart+near+84108&CTS=Pet+Grooming&R=D&MCBP=true&F=1';
// Generate a distance sort link:
var url='http://yellowpages.superpages.com/listings.jsp?C=petsmart+near+84108&CTS=Pet+Grooming&R=D&EG=1&MCBP=true&OO=1&F=1'+rrvalue+ppvalue;

yexturl = "http://pl.yext.com/pljs?pid=2cd0f1d10f&event=serp_impression";
yextids = "1720388";
get_yextag();
yext_click(yextids,'impression')
function get_yextag(){
$.getJSON(yexturl + '&ids=' + yextids + '&callback=?',
function(jd) {
$.each(jd, function(i,item){
yext_tag(this,item);
});
});
}
function yext_tag(i,datos) {
//var div = $("#yext_" + datos.yextId);
//var divc = $("#yextc_" + datos.yextId);
/*
* to support rendering of multiple elemetnt with same id above code got blocked
* and below code change got introduced. IR01809074
*/
var div = $("span[id=yext_" + datos.yextId+"]");
var divc = $("span[id=yextc_" + datos.yextId+"]");
for (var j = 0; j <div.length; j++){
var ytag = "";
var soUrl = datos.specialOffer.url;
var clickBP = $(div[j]).attr('onClick');
$(div[j]).removeAttr('title');
if(datos.specialOffer.message != "") {
datatag = "";
dt = datos.specialOffer.message;
dl = dt.length;
did = datos.yextId;
dtle = dt;
dtle = dtle.replace(/'/g, "&#039;");
if(dl > 19){ datatag = dt.substring(0,16) + "..."; }else{ datatag = dt; }
//ytag = "<div class='yext-tag' style='float:left;min-width:100px;margin-top:5px;white-space: pre-line;'> ";
ytag = "<p class='yext-tag' id='yext-tag"+ j + "' > ";
if(soUrl) {
var dtrack = '{"title":"Yext Special Offer"}';
ytag = ytag + "<a href='" + soUrl + "' id='yext-link"+ j + "' data-track='" + dtrack + "' onClick='yext_click(\"" + did + "\",\"click\");' target='_blank' title='"+ dtle +"'>";
}
ytagc = ytag + unescape(dt);
ytag = ytag + unescape(datatag);
if(soUrl != ""){ //ytag = ytag + "</a></div>";
ytag = ytag + "</a></p>";
$(div[j]).html(ytagc);
$(divc[j]).html(ytag);
} else {
$(divc[j]).css("display","none");
}
}
}
}
function yext_click(id,act){
// NOTE: clicks are routed through Yext for click tracking
var target = "";
var pagesrc="serp";
if(act == "click"){
target = "&target=specialoffer";
}
var selectedcategory = "petsmart";
var clickurl = 'http://pl.yext.com/plpixel?pid=2cd0f1d10f&source='+ pagesrc +'&action=' + act + target + '&ids=' +
id + '&query=' + selectedcategory + '&property=superpages.com';
var img = document.createElement('img');
img.src = clickurl;
img.width = "1";
img.height = "1";
document.getElementsByTagName('body')[0].appendChild(img);
}

var itemIDNumber=0;
var itemFL="FL=top";
// multiple links on the page may the same overlay div.
// these functions display/hide the overlay in a position relative to the links
// (the links are moreN and lessN, where N is itemNumber)
// and hide or show those links as appropriate
// we also sets up logging, so we can distinguish clicks on different links (by fl param)
function showListingsOverlay(itemNumber, fl)
{
// since we have a link to display this in multiple places, a user may scroll around
// and click from multiple places. so if overlay was already displayed - hide it and reset the link to display it
hideListingsOverlay();
// these two vars are defined above and are set here for use in closing!
itemIDNumber=itemNumber;
itemFL=fl;
var ref = document.getElementById('less'+itemIDNumber);
var div = document.getElementById('listingsOverlay');
// if we are at the top, display overlay just below the link
if (itemFL=='FL=top')
moveElement(div, ref, 20);
else {
// this is the link at the bottom, get the height and place the overlay just above the link
var myHeight = 40;
if (div.currentStyle) { //ie way
myHeight = div.offsetHeight;
}
if (window.getComputedStyle) { //mozilla way
var myElementCS = document.defaultView.getComputedStyle(div, null);
myHeight = parseInt(myElementCS.getPropertyValue('height'));
}
moveElement(div, ref, -(myHeight));
}
overlay('listingsOverlay');
hideform('less'+itemIDNumber);
showform('dvmore'+itemIDNumber);
}
function hideListingsOverlay()
{
hideoverlay('listingsOverlay');
hideform('dvmore'+itemIDNumber);
showform('less'+itemIDNumber);
}
function moveElement(el, ref, topOff)
{
var referTop = ref.offsetTop;
var tempRef = ref;
while(tempRef.offsetParent){
tempRef = tempRef.offsetParent;
referTop += tempRef.offsetTop;
}
el.style.top = referTop + topOff;
}
// change the logging params to reflect which link was clicked
function setFL(href)
{
return href.replace("FL=top", itemFL);
}
// -->

<script language="JavaScript" type="text/javascript">
function BrowserCheck() {
var b = navigator.appName;
if (b == "Netscape") this.b = "NS";
else if (b == "Microsoft Internet Explorer") this.b = "IE";
else this.b = b;
this.v = parseInt(navigator.appVersion);
this.NS = (this.b == "NS" && this.v>=4);
this.NS4 = (this.b == "NS" && this.v == 4);
this.NS5 = (this.b == "NS" && this.v == 5);
this.IE = (this.b == "IE" && this.v>=4);
this.IE4 = (navigator.userAgent.indexOf('MSIE 4')>0);
this.IE5 = (navigator.userAgent.indexOf('MSIE 5')>0);
if (this.IE5 || this.NS5) this.VER5 = true;
if (this.IE4 || this.NS4) this.VER4 = true;
this.OLD = (! this.VER5 && ! this.VER4) ? true : false;
this.min = (this.NS||this.IE);
}
is = new BrowserCheck();
alertBox = (is.VER5) ? document.getElementById("alertLayer").style
: (is.NS) ? document.layers["alertLayer"]
: document.all["alertLayer"].style;
$(document).ready(function() {
if (mapable==true){
$("#myMap").css("position", "relative");
$("#myMap").css('border-bottom', '6px solid #677580');
}else{
$("#myMap").css("position", "absolute");
$("#myMap").css('border', 0 +'px');
}
var offset = 220;
var duration = 10;
jQuery(window).scroll(function() {
if (jQuery(this).scrollTop() > offset) {
jQuery('.back-to-top').fadeIn(duration);
} else {
jQuery('.back-to-top').fadeOut(duration);
}
});
jQuery('.back-to-top').click(function(event) {
event.preventDefault();
jQuery('html, body').animate({scrollTop: 0}, duration);
return false;
})
});

function readCookie(name) {
var nameEQ = name + "=";
var ca = document.cookie.split(';');
for(var i=0;i < ca.length;i++) {
var c = ca[i];
while (c.charAt(0)==' ') c = c.substring(1,c.length);
if (c.indexOf(nameEQ) == 0)
if (c.indexOf(nameEQ) == 0) return c.substring(nameEQ.length,c.length);
}
}

var state = escape(document.hiddenform.S.value);
var starting_point= escape(document.hiddenform.AL.value);
var sort= escape(document.hiddenform.R.value);
var pagesize= escape(document.hiddenform.PS.value);
var resultradius= escape(document.hiddenform.RR.value);

}
}
if(location != null && location =="")

if(var_lastquery_state != "")

}
if(var_lastquery_zip != "")
{
if(location != "")
location+='+';
location+=var_lastquery_zip;
}
}
if(location == "USA" || location =="usa")
location = "";
if (arg_stype == "" && form_stype != "") {
var stype = form_stype;
} else {
var stype = arg_stype;
}

// this condition is only for the mabtab on the advanced search form
var pageName = "yp_error";
if(stype == "M" && (pagesize == null || pagesize == "") && pageName == "yp_detail_form")

else

if ( (document.ypform && document.ypform.L) || (document.hiddenform && document.hiddenform.L)) {
str += "&L="+location;
}
if (stype == "D") {
str += "&RE="+street+"&RT="+city+"&RS="+state+"&RZ="+zip;
}else if(stype == "M" && newmaps == "true"){
str += "&L="+location+"&SRC="+src;
}
else {
str += "&E="+street+"&T="+city+"&S="+state+"&Z="+zip;
}
} else {
var str="?SRC=&#38;STYPE=S&#38;PG=L&#38;R=N&#38;C=&#38;N=&#38;T=&#38;S="
}
return str;
}

/* returns the value of the name cookie */
function readCookie(name) {
var nameEQ = name + "=";
var ca = document.cookie.split(';');
for(var i=0;i < ca.length;i++) {
var c = ca[i];

}
}

}
} else if(document.ypform.RS) {

var state = escape(document.hiddenform.S.value);

/* returns the value of the name cookie */
function readCookie(name) {
var nameEQ = name + "=";
var ca = document.cookie.split(';');
for(var i=0;i < ca.length;i++) {
var c = ca[i];
while (c.charAt(0)==' ') c = c.substring(1,c.length);
if (c.indexOf(nameEQ) == 0)
if (c.indexOf(nameEQ) == 0) return c.substring(nameEQ.length,c.length);
}
}

/* returns the value of the name cookie */
function readCookie(name) {
var nameEQ = name + "=";
var ca = document.cookie.split(';');
for(var i=0;i < ca.length;i++) {
var c = ca[i];
while (c.charAt(0)==' ') c = c.substring(1,c.length);
if (c.indexOf(nameEQ) == 0)
if (c.indexOf(nameEQ) == 0) return c.substring(nameEQ.length,c.length);
}
}

function getfeatures(id,mp,yextTagId, listingNumber) {
var hc = false;
var inx = 0;
var yextTagDivArray = $("div[id=yext-tag" + yextTagId+"]");
//var yextag = $("#yext-tag" + id).clone();
var yextag = $(yextTagDivArray[0]).clone();
var features = $("<div class='coupons'></div>");
if(id != 0){
if($("#fl" + id).length == 1){
var morefeat = $("#mofe" + id).clone();
features = $(features).append($("#fl" + id).clone());
$('li',features).each(function(index) {
inx = index + 1;
if((yextag.length == 1 && morefeat)){ hc=true; }
if ($(this).is("#coupon" + id) || $(this).is("#of" + id))
{
$(this).css("float","left"); $(this).css("display","block"); $(this).css("margin-left","-2px"); hc=true;
} else { $(this).remove(); }
});
if(inx > 0){ fltp = 3; }
if(morefeat && mp!=1){
$(morefeat.html()).appendTo($(features));
}
if(!hc && !yextag){ $("#dmf" + id).remove(); }
$(".feature-links",features).css("margin","0");
$(".feature-links",features).css("padding","0");
}
}else{
/* when pinTag value is not available for a listing,
at that mofe and f1 div is not renedering with proper id in listingpage.links.jsf.
For that reason it's require to retrieve mofe and f1 div as a children of mpbtm div.
*/
var morefeat = $("#mpbtm" + listingNumber).children("div.coupons").children("#mofe");
var fl = $("#mpbtm" + listingNumber).children("div.coupons").children("#fl");
features = $(features).append($(fl).clone());
$('li',features).each(function(index) {
inx = index + 1;
if((yextag.length == 1 && morefeat)){ hc=true; }
if ($(this).is("#coupon") || $(this).is("#of"))
{
$(this).css("float","left"); $(this).css("display","block"); $(this).css("margin-left","-2px"); hc=true;
} else { $(this).remove(); }
});
if(inx > 0){ fltp = 3; }
if(morefeat && mp!=1){
$(morefeat.html()).appendTo($(features));
}
if(!hc && !yextag){
$("#dmf" + (listingNumber+1)).remove();
}
$(".feature-links",features).css("margin","0");
$(".feature-links",features).css("padding","0");
}
if(yextag){
$(".yext-t",yextag).css("margin","4px 0 0 0");
$(".yext-t",yextag).css("float","left");
$(".yext-t",yextag).css("display","block");
$(".yextall",yextag).css("display","none");
$(".yexttrim",yextag).css("display","block");
$(yextag.html()).prependTo($(features));
}
if($("#fl" + id).length == 1 || yextag){
return features.html();
} else {
return;
}
}

//console.log("enter gbplc id: " + id);

if (clone) {
var text = $('.detailName',clone).text();

$(".listResults",clone).after("<div class='addressDetails'>"+adds+"</div>");
$(".vlst",clone).after("<p style='float:left;padding-top:15px;clear:both'><a onclick='"+moreInfo+"'" + " href='"+mInfohref+"'>More Info</a></p>");
//console.info(adds);

$("#reviewimagediv",clone).remove();
$(".reviewtext1",clone).remove();
$(".links",clone).remove();
$(".icons",clone).remove();
$(".business-text",clone).remove();
$(".phone",clone).remove();
$(".listingNumber",clone).remove();

var addh = $('.address',clone).outerHeight();

$(".addressDetails",clone).css("top", bush + "px");
$("#flyoutDiv .reviews",clone).css("top", rewh + "px");
}
var clnHtml = clone.html();
//console.log("clnHtml: " + clnHtml);
var trackingAttrWithMap = 'data-track=\'{\"inmap\":\"true\",';
if ($.browser.msie) {

clnHtml = clnHtml.replace(trackingAttr, trackingAttrWithMap);
}
else {
var addMapIndEnd = '}\'';
//clnHtml = clnHtml.replace(/data-track=\"{/g,trackingAttrWithMap);
//clnHtml = clnHtml.replace(/}\"/g,addMapIndEnd);
}
return fltp + "spFlyoutType" + "<section class=\"listings\" style=\"width:auto;padding-bottom:0px;margin-bottom:0px;\"><article style=\"padding:0px;border-bottom:none;\">"+clnHtml + "</article></section>";
}
function hlListing(n) {
var a = document.getElementsByTagName("article");
for (var i = 1; i < a.length; i++) {

if (e) {
if (n == i){
e.css("background-color","#DBEBF2");
} else {
e.css("background-color","");
}
}
}
}

var itemIDNumber=0;
var itemFL="FL=top";
// multiple links on the page may the same overlay div.
// these functions display/hide the overlay in a position relative to the links
// (the links are moreN and lessN, where N is itemNumber)
// and hide or show those links as appropriate
// we also sets up logging, so we can distinguish clicks on different links (by fl param)
function showListingsOverlay(itemNumber, fl)
{
// since we have a link to display this in multiple places, a user may scroll around
// and click from multiple places. so if overlay was already displayed - hide it and reset the link to display it
hideListingsOverlay();
// these two vars are defined above and are set here for use in closing!

itemFL=fl;
var ref = document.getElementById('less'+itemIDNumber);
var div = document.getElementById('listingsOverlay');
// if we are at the top, display overlay just below the link
if (itemFL=='FL=top')
moveElement(div, ref, 20);
else {
// this is the link at the bottom, get the height and place the overlay just above the link
var myHeight = 40;
if (div.currentStyle) { //ie way
myHeight = div.offsetHeight;
}
if (window.getComputedStyle) { //mozilla way
var myElementCS = document.defaultView.getComputedStyle(div, null);
myHeight = parseInt(myElementCS.getPropertyValue('height'));
}
moveElement(div, ref, -(myHeight));
}
overlay('listingsOverlay');
hideform('less'+itemIDNumber);
showform('dvmore'+itemIDNumber);
}
function hideListingsOverlay()
{
hideoverlay('listingsOverlay');
hideform('dvmore'+itemIDNumber);
showform('less'+itemIDNumber);
}
function moveElement(el, ref, topOff)
{
var referTop = ref.offsetTop;
var tempRef = ref;
while(tempRef.offsetParent){
tempRef = tempRef.offsetParent;
referTop += tempRef.offsetTop;
}
el.style.top = referTop + topOff;
}
// change the logging params to reflect which link was clicked
function setFL(href)
{
return href.replace("FL=top", itemFL);
}

<script language="JavaScript" type="text/javascript">
function BrowserCheck() {
var b = navigator.appName;
if (b == "Netscape") this.b = "NS";
else if (b == "Microsoft Internet Explorer") this.b = "IE";
else this.b = b;
this.v = parseInt(navigator.appVersion);
this.NS = (this.b == "NS" && this.v>=4);
this.NS4 = (this.b == "NS" && this.v == 4);
this.NS5 = (this.b == "NS" && this.v == 5);
this.IE = (this.b == "IE" && this.v>=4);
this.IE4 = (navigator.userAgent.indexOf('MSIE 4')>0);
this.IE5 = (navigator.userAgent.indexOf('MSIE 5')>0);
if (this.IE5 || this.NS5) this.VER5 = true;
if (this.IE4 || this.NS4) this.VER4 = true;
this.OLD = (! this.VER5 && ! this.VER4) ? true : false;
this.min = (this.NS||this.IE);
}
is = new BrowserCheck();
alertBox = (is.VER5) ? document.getElementById("alertLayer").style
: (is.NS) ? document.layers["alertLayer"]
: document.all["alertLayer"].style;

var offset = 220;
var duration = 10;
jQuery(window).scroll(function() {
if (jQuery(this).scrollTop() > offset) {
jQuery('.back-to-top').fadeIn(duration);
} else {
jQuery('.back-to-top').fadeOut(duration);
}
});
jQuery('.back-to-top').click(function(event) {
event.preventDefault();
jQuery('html, body').animate({scrollTop: 0}, duration);
return false;
})
});
